 # mamahadia post shared by Puspa Dewi (@puspadewihc) on Oct 4, 2017 at 7:46am PDT The current Bharatiya Janata Party central government came to power in 2014 with several big promises, one of which was the promise of cleaning the Ganges
 lekin abhi bhi ganga kaa haal vaisaa hi lagata he
 Regarding the river Ganges flowing over 2,071 kilometers in the country, the World Wildlife Fund says that the Ganges is one of the most endangered rivers in the world because almost all the other Indian rivers, like the first continuous flood and then drought in the Ganges a situation is arising
 uttarakhand main himalay se lekar bengal kii khadi ke sundarbans tak ganga vishaal bhu-bhaag ko sinchati he
 The Ganges forms a vast fertile plain covering an area of 1 million square kilometers with its tributaries of 2,071 km in India and then Bangladesh
 ganga nadi ke raste main padane vaale rajyon main uttarakhand, uttar pradesh, bihar, jharkhand or pashchim bengal shaamil hai
 The major tributaries coming from the north in the Ganga are Yamuna, Ramganga, Karnali (ghaghra), Tapti, Gandak, Kosi and Kakshi, while the major rivers coming from the plateau of the south are Chambal, Son, Betwa, Cane, Southern
 Tos etc
 yamuna ganga kii sabase pramukh sahaayak nadi he, jo himalay kii bandarpunch chotii ke yamunotri himkhand se nikalati he
 The Ganges joins the Bay of Bengal covering 110 km in Uttarakhand, 1,450 km in Uttar Pradesh, 445 km in Bihar and 520 km in West Bengal
 ganga kaa aadhyatmik mahatv
 
 
 The Ganges also has spiritual and cultural significance in our texts
 granthon ke mutabik, ganga kaa arth he, bahna
 Ganga is the identity of India and is also a fundamental door that binds the spiritual and cultural values of the country
 desh ke sabase pavitra sthanon main shumaar rishikesh, haridwar, prayag or kaashi, ganga ke tat par sthit hai
 Apart from this, Kedarnath, Badrinath and Gomukh are among the pilgrimage places along the banks of Ganga and its tributaries
 jin chaar sthanon par kumbh mela lagata he, unamem se do shahar haridwar or prayag ganga tat par sthit hai
 Where the dirt is spreading
 
 
 samachar agency IANS dwaara jari report ke mutabik, jahaan takpradooshanki baat he to ganga rishikesh se hi pradooshit ho rahi he

 isliye yah gandagi bhi ganga main mil rahi he, kanpur kii ore 400 kimi ulataa jane par ganga kii dasha sabase dayaneey dikhti he

 ) Long-term intake of high doses of common painkillers increases the risk of heart attack
 in dawaaon kaa seven kar rahe 350,000 se bhi zyada marijon par kiye gaye ek adhyayan main paaya gaya ki unamem heart atake kaa khatra 40 fisadi zyada he
 According to the study, the use of painkillers such as ibuprofen can be as dangerous as the Vox drug, which has already been banned worldwide a decade ago
 research main paaya gaya tha ki vioks ke seven se heart atake kaa jokhim doguna ho jaataa he
